  </h4>
  
     <p> Coniferous trees shroud the trail, snowy boughs creaking beneath the weight of their wintery burden. A single post marks a fork in the ancient road, the signage weathered beyond legibility. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('mH618BGC');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Several caravans are circling a large camp fire on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail.      <p> The trees here are naked and twisted. Their branches reach down like bony claws. Was this place cursed in days long gone? </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('08TPZJf9');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> <strong> 3 Werebears</strong> are wandering next to a clearing. </p> <p> Theres a <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d6' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d6');"><strong>2-in-6</strong></a> chance of encountering at least some of them outside (the rest will be in their lair inside an old forgotten gold mine). </p> <p> <strong>Werebear</strong>   <hr/> <div id="block-08TPZJf9" class="monster-block"> <div class="statblock"> <div class="statblock-top-row"> <div><span class="section-label">CR:</span> 5 (1800 XP)</div> <div><span class="section-label">AC:</span> 10in humanoid form,11 (natural armor)in bear or hybrid form</div> <div><span class="section-label">HP:</span>  (18d8 + 54)</div> <div><span class="section-label">Speed:</span> Walk 30 ft. (40 ft., climb 30 ft. in bear or hybrid form)</div> </div> <table class="statblock-table"> <tr><th>STR</th><th>DEX</th><th>CON</th><th>INT</th><th>WIS</th><th>CHA</th></tr> <tr> <td>19 <small> +5 </small> </td> <td>10 <small>  </small> </td> <td>17 <small> +4 </small> </td> <td>11 <small> +1 </small> </td> <td>12 <small> +1 </small> </td> <td>12 <small> +1 </small> </td> </tr> </table> <div> <input class="monster-block-toggle" name="toggle-08TPZJf9" id="toggle-08TPZJf9" type="checkbox" onclick="javascript:document.getElementById('block-08TPZJf9').scrollIntoView();"/> <div id="block-toggle-08TPZJf9" class="statblock-container"> <ul>   <li><strong>Immunities: </strong> ; bludgeoning, piercing and slashing from nonmagical attacks that aren't silvered</li>    <li><strong>Alignment: </strong> Neutral Good</li>   <li><strong>Languages: </strong> Common (can't speak in bear form)</li>  </ul>  <hr/> <div><ul> <li><strong>Shapechanger:</strong> The werebear can use its action to polymorph into a Large bear-humanoid hybrid or into a Large bear, or back into its true form, which is humanoid. Its statistics, other than its size and AC, are the same in each form. Any equipment it is wearing or carrying isn't transformed.      <p> So big and tall are the trees here. Their tops are almost hidden by the dense mist. Their trunks are as wide as a hut. Some of them have planks of wood attached, forming a ladder. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('wDlK7lnH');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Theres a magical portal to another hex deep in the woods.       <p> The Swords Of Justice militia are conspiring to overthrow the ruler of the realm. </p>  <p> The militias usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/Fw0E6HFn"><strong>"The Bleeding Pixie Tavern"</strong></a> in <strong>Heartseeker Forest</strong> </p> 
      <p> The militia leader is a <strong>Caloanna of Palemoon</strong>, a level 6 Dwarf Fighter.  She has heavy makeup, crystal blue eyes and chubby cheeks (<em>Distressed</em>).    Caloanna has a special interest of an unknown nature in <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/tgN97l5c/npc/sl6mtOjr"><strong>Walo of Dorith</strong></a> .  </p> <strong>Caloanna of Palemoon</strong>
